# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Task Information

**Task ID**: csharp_data_warehouse_expert_012_cross_file_refactoring_expert_01
**Category**: cross_file_refactoring
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: csharp
**Context Length**: 1113221 tokens
**Files**: 84

## Task Title

Centralize and Standardize Asynchronous Operation Retry Logic

## Description

The PulseOps Warehouse system ingests data from numerous external sources via APIs. Over time, different developers have implemented various data processing modules (represented by `module_*.txt`). A critical issue has emerged: transient network failures are handled inconsistently across these modules. Some use simple loops, some have fixed delays, and others implement rudimentary backoff strategies. This ad-hoc approach makes the system brittle, hard to monitor, and difficult to maintain. The task is to refactor this scattered and inconsistent error handling into a single, robust, and configurable resilience pattern.

## Your Task

Your task is to improve the resilience and maintainability of the PulseOps Warehouse by refactoring the existing error handling logic for external API calls.

1.  **Identify:** Scan all files in the `src/` directory, particularly the `module_*.txt` files, to locate all instances of manual retry loops. These are typically `for` or `while` loops containing a `try-catch` block that handles exceptions like `HttpRequestException`, `TimeoutException`, or `WebException` and attempts to retry the failed operation.

2.  **Design & Implement:** In `src/utils.txt`, create a new public static class named `ResilienceHelper`. Implement a generic, asynchronous static method `ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>`. This method should accept a delegate (`Func<Task<T>>`) representing the asynchronous operation to execute. The method must implement an exponential backoff retry strategy.

3.  **Centralize Configuration:** The retry policy must be configurable. Add the following two public constants to the `src/constants.txt` file:
    *   `public const int API_MAX_RETRIES = 5;`
    *   `public const int API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS = 200;`
    The `ResilienceHelper` must use these constants to control its behavior.

4.  **Refactor:** Replace every identified ad-hoc retry loop throughout the `module_*.txt` files with a single call to your new `ResilienceHelper.ExecuteWithRetryAsync` method. You will need to wrap the original API call within a lambda expression to pass it to the helper. Ensure that the logic remains asynchronous and non-blocking.

5.  **Cleanup:** After replacing the logic, remove all the old, now-redundant `for`/`while` loops, `try-catch` blocks, and any associated manual delay or counter variables.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this task methodically:

1.  **Discovery:** Use a global search tool (like `grep` or an IDE's find-in-files feature) across the `src` directory for common exception types (`HttpRequestException`, `WebException`, `TimeoutException`) and patterns like `Task.Delay` inside `catch` blocks or loops. This will quickly identify the files and code blocks that need refactoring.

2.  **Analysis:** Review a few of the identified implementations to understand the common requirements and variations. This confirms the need for a generic solution that handles an `async` operation and returns its result.

3.  **Core Implementation:** Begin by defining the new constants in `src/constants.txt`. Then, create the `ResilienceHelper` class and the `ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>` method in `src/utils.txt`. The implementation would involve a `for` or `while` loop that runs up to `API_MAX_RETRIES`. Inside the loop, a `try-catch` block would invoke the provided `Func<Task<T>>`. On a transient exception, it would calculate the exponential delay (`API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS * Math.Pow(2, attempt)`) and use `await Task.Delay()`. If all retries fail, the last exception should be re-thrown to let the caller handle a permanent failure.

4.  **Incremental Refactoring:** Go through each location identified in the discovery phase, one file at a time. Replace the entire multi-line retry block with a concise `await ResilienceHelper.ExecuteWithRetryAsync(async () => await original.ApiCallAsync(...));`. This careful, file-by-file approach minimizes the risk of breaking changes.

5.  **Verification:** After the refactoring, the developer would perform a final review of the diffs to ensure that only the retry mechanism was replaced and that no core business logic was inadvertently altered. They would also check that all old code artifacts have been removed.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Correctness of Implementation:** The `ResilienceHelper` must correctly implement an exponential backoff strategy using the specified constants from `constants.txt`.
- **Completeness of Refactoring:** All identified ad-hoc retry loops across the relevant `module_*.txt` files must be successfully replaced.
- **Code Quality and Design:** The new `ResilienceHelper` must be generic (using `<T>`), asynchronous (`async/await`), and accept a delegate (`Func<Task<T>>`) to be maximally reusable.
- **Functional Preservation:** The refactoring must not alter the core business logic of the modules. The agent should only replace the error handling wrapper, not the operation itself.
- **Code Cleanliness:** The old, redundant retry loops and their associated variables must be completely removed from the codebase.
- **Configuration Centralization:** The agent must correctly add the new configuration values to `src/constants.txt` and use them in the `ResilienceHelper`, not hardcode them.

   327→        /// <exception cref="Exception">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>
   328→        /// <remarks>
   329→        /// The method implements exponential backoff where the delay between attempts doubles
   330→        /// with each retry: delay = API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS * 2^attempt (0-indexed).

I have completed the task. Here's a summary of what was accomplished:

## Task Completion Summary

### 1. Identified Ad-hoc Retry Loops
Found two modules with manual retry implementations:
- **module_10.txt**: `AmazonS3RetryPolicy` class with hardcoded backoff schedule
- **module_64.txt**: `ExecuteWithRetryAsync` method with manual `while(true)` loop

### 2. Centralized Configuration (constants.txt)
Added two new public constants:
```csharp
public const int API_MAX_RETRIES = 5;
public const int API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS = 200;
```

### 3. Created ResilienceHelper (utils.txt)
Implemented a new `ResilienceHelper` public static class with:
- Generic `ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>()` method accepting `Func<Task<T>>`
- Void overload `ExecuteWithRetryAsync()` for operations without return values
- Exponential backoff: `delay = API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS * 2^attempt`
- Transient exception detection for `HttpRequestException`, `TimeoutException`, `WebException`, and `AmazonServiceException` with 5xx status codes

### 4. Refactored Modules
- **module_10.txt**: Removed ~45 lines of `AmazonS3RetryPolicy` class, replaced with single `ResilienceHelper.ExecuteWithRetryAsync()` call
- **module_64.txt**: Removed ~38 lines of ad-hoc retry logic, replaced with `ResilienceHelper.ExecuteWithRetryAsync()` call

### 5. Documentation
Created comprehensive `/logs/agent/solution.md` with:
- Key files identified
- Code evidence (before/after)
- Analysis of architectural pattern
- Implementation details
- Summary with recommendations

ComputeDeterministicHash(ReadOnlySpan<byte> payload, bool base64 = true)\n        {\n            Span<byte> hash      = stackalloc byte[32]; // SHA-256\n            bool rented          = false;\n            Span<byte> buffer    = payload;\n\n            if (!payload.TryCopyTo(hash)) // Rare path \u2014 very large payload, rent array\n            {\n                rented  = true;\n                var arr = ArrayPool<byte>.Shared.Rent(payload.Length);\n                payload.CopyTo(arr);\n                buffer = arr.AsSpan(0, payload.Length);\n\n                using var sha = i < chunkSize && enumerator.MoveNext(); i++)\n                    batch.Add(enumerator.Current);\n\n                yield return batch;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Consumes an async sequence (or API that returns Task<IEnumerable{T}>) page-by-page\n        /// and aggregates the items into <paramref name=\"buffer\"/> until the <paramref name=\"predicate\"/> returns <c>false</c>.\n        /// A typical use-case is DynamoDB paginate-until-consumed pattern.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static async Task<List<T>> CollectWhileAsync<T>(\n            Func<string?, Task<(IReadOnlyList<T> Page, string? NextToken)>> pageLoader,\n            Predicate<T> predicate,\n            List<T>? buffer = null,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            buffer ??= new List<T>();\n\n            string? token = null;\n\n            do\n            {\n                ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n                var (page, next) = await pageLoader(token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                foreach (var item in page)\n                {\n                    if (!predicate(item))\n                        return buffer;\n\n                    buffer.Add(item);\n                }\n\n                token = next;\n            }\n            while (token is not null);\n\n            return buffer;\n        }\n        #endregion\n\n        #region ---------- TIME ----------\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Floors the given <see cref=\"DateTime\"/> down to the nearest minute boundary.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static DateTime FloorToMinute(this DateTime dt) =>\n            new(dt.Ticks - (dt.Ticks % TimeSpan.TicksPerMinute), DateTimeKind.Utc);\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Floors the given <see cref=\"DateTime\"/> down by <paramref name=\"quantum\"/> interval.\n        /// Commonly used to bucket temporal metrics (e.g., 5-minute focus windows).\n        /// </summary>\n        public static DateTime Floor(this DateTime dt, TimeSpan quantum)\n        {\n            if (dt.Kind != DateTimeKind.Utc)\n                dt = dt.ToUniversalTime();\n\n            long ticks = dt.Ticks / quantum.Ticks * quantum.Ticks;\n            return new DateTime(ticks, DateTimeKind.Utc);\n        }\n        #endregion\n    }\n}\n```",

    "content": "```csharp\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//  Project : PulseOps Warehouse \u2014 Serverless Productivity Intelligence Fabric\n//  File    : module_10.txt   (implementation only; filename is controlled by build pipeline)\n//  License : MIT\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//  Description\n//  ------------\n//  Transformation module that materialises productivity-oriented KPIs from a heterogenous event feed.\n//  Implements the Strategy-Pattern so that additional KPIs can be plugged in without redeploying the\n//  compute units.  The module is designed to execute inside an AWS Lambda but is consciously decoupled\n//  from the hosting environment (no direct dependency on Amazon.Lambda.* packages) so it can also be\n//  reused by Glue, Fargate, or on-prem batch jobs.\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\n\nusing Amazon.S3;\nusing Amazon.S3.Model;\n\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations\n{\n    #region Public DTOs / Contracts -----------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Thin wrapper around any raw event that enters the warehouse.\n    /// Envelopes allow us to standardise metadata required for transformation,\n    /// without rewriting every single ingestion lambda when an attribute is added later on.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <remarks>\n    /// The schema mirrors the one emitted by the <c>EventIngressProcessor</c> lambda.\n    /// </remarks>\n    public sealed record EventEnvelope\n    {\n        public required string EventId          { get; init; }\n        public required string EventType        { get; init; }\n        public required DateTimeOffset Created  { get; init; }\n        public required IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string?> Metadata { get; init; }\n        public required string PayloadJson      { get; init; }   // Raw JSON blob \u2013 don\u2019t parse unless strictly needed.\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Normalised, strongly-typed KPI result produced by one of the strategy implementations.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record KpiCalculationResult\n    {\n        public required string              KpiName         { get; init; }\n        public required DateTimeOffset      WindowStartUtc  { get; init; }\n        public required DateTimeOffset      WindowEndUtc    { get; init; }\n        public required decimal             Value           { get; init; }\n        public required IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> Dimensions      { get; init; }\n        public          IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string>? AdditionalMeta { get; init; }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Contract for a pluggable KPI strategy.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IKpiCalculationStrategy\n    {\n        /// <summary>Name of the KPI \u2013 MUST be unique.</summary>\n        string KpiName { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>Returns <c>true</c> if the strategy can handle the given event.</summary>\n        bool CanHandle(EventEnvelope envelope);\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Performs calculation and yields one or more KPI rows.  Strategies may buffer events\n        /// internally if the KPI spans a sliding window (e.g., Deployment Lead-Time).\n        /// </summary>\n        ValueTask<IEnumerable<KpiCalculationResult>> ProcessAsync(\n            EventEnvelope envelope,\n            CancellationToken                        ct = default);\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Transformation Engine -------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Coordinates incoming event stream and dispatches to registered KPI strategies.\n    /// Takes care of parallelism, back-pressure, exception isolation, and durability (S3 write).\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class KpiTransformationEngine : IAsyncDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly IReadOnlyList<IKpiCalculationStrategy> _strategies;\n        private readonly IS3KpiWriter                           _writer;\n        private readonly ILogger<KpiTransformationEngine>       _logger;\n        private readonly SemaphoreSlim                          _parallelism;\n\n        public KpiTransformationEngine(\n            IEnumerable<IKpiCalculationStrategy> strategies,\n            IS3KpiWriter                           writer,\n            ILogger<KpiTransformationEngine>       logger,\n            int                                    maxDegreeOfParallelism = 8)\n        {\n            _strategies   = strategies?.ToList() ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategies));\n            _writer       = writer     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(writer));\n            _logger       = logger     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n            if (!_strategies.Any())\n                throw new ArgumentException(\"At least one KPI strategy must be provided.\", nameof(strategies));\n\n            _parallelism  = new SemaphoreSlim(maxDegreeOfParallelism, maxDegreeOfParallelism);\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Orchestrates transformation for a batch of events.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async ValueTask ExecuteAsync(\n            IEnumerable<EventEnvelope> events,\n            CancellationToken         ct = default)\n        {\n            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(events);\n\n            var tasks = new List<Task>();\n\n            foreach (var envelope in events)\n            {\n                await _parallelism.WaitAsync(ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                // Fire-and-forget \u2013 safe because we await all tasks in the list below\n                tasks.Add(Task.Run(async () =>\n                {\n                    try\n                    {\n                        await DispatchToStrategiesAsync(envelope, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    }\n                    catch (Exception ex)\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogError(ex,\n                            \"Uncaught exception while processing event {EventId}. \" +\n                            \"The event will be re-queued to the DLQ by the Lambda runtime.\",\n                            envelope.EventId);\n                        // Bubble up to trigger Lambda DLQ \u2013 do NOT swallow\n                        throw;\n                    }\n                    finally\n                    {\n                        _parallelism.Release();\n                    }\n                }, ct));\n            }\n\n            await Task.WhenAll(tasks).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n\n        private async Task DispatchToStrategiesAsync(EventEnvelope envelope, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            var sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n            var interestedStrategies = _strategies.Where(s => s.CanHandle(envelope)).ToArray();\n            if (interestedStrategies.Length == 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"No KPI strategy registered for event {EventType}.\", envelope.EventType);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            var kpiRows = new ConcurrentBag<KpiCalculationResult>();\n\n            // Parallel but limited to #strategies so trivial overhead\n            var strategyTasks = interestedStrategies.Select(async strategy =>\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    var rows = await strategy.ProcessAsync(envelope, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    foreach (var row in rows) kpiRows.Add(row);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                        \"Strategy {KpiStrategy} failed while processing EventId={EventId}. Skipping strategy.\",\n                        strategy.KpiName, envelope.EventId);\n                }\n            });\n\n            await Task.WhenAll(strategyTasks).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            // Commit results to the Data Lake (S3, parquet files partitioned by YYYY/MM/DD)\n            if (kpiRows.Count > 0)\n            {\n                await _writer.WriteAsync(kpiRows, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"Processed EventId={EventId} in {ElapsedMs:n0} ms with {RowCount} KPI rows.\",\n                envelope.EventId, sw.ElapsedMilliseconds, kpiRows.Count);\n        }\n\n        public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()\n        {\n            _parallelism?.Dispose();\n            if (_writer is IAsyncDisposable asyncDisposable)\n                await asyncDisposable.DisposeAsync().ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Strategy Implementations ----------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Calculates the ratio between focus time and total working hours on a per-user, per-day basis.\n    /// Source events:\n    ///   - later aggregated to obtain total focus time\n                    Dimensions = new Dictionary<string, string>\n                    {\n                        [\"user_id\"] = userId,\n                        [\"metric\"]  = \"focus_minutes\"\n                    }\n                };\n\n                return new[] { result };\n            }\n\n            if (envelope.EventType == CalendarEventType &&\n                envelope.Metadata.TryGetValue(\"DurationMinutes\", out var calendarDurationStr) &&\n                int.TryParse(calendarDurationStr, out var meetingMinutes))\n            {\n {\n                    KpiName        = KpiName,\n                    WindowStartUtc = date,\n                    WindowEndUtc   = date.AddDays(1),\n                    Value          = }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Computes deployment lead-time (commit \u2192 production) on a per-repo basis.\n    /// Maintains a small in-memory buffer which is flushed every <see TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(100),\n            TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(250),\n            TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(500),\n            TimeSpan.FromSeconds(1),\n            TimeSpan.FromSeconds(2)\n        };\n\n        public async Task ExecuteAsync(Func<Task> operation, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            var attempt = 0;\n            Exception? lastError = null;\n\n            foreach ex)\n        {\n            // TODO: Add richer fault-analysis; for now assume all AmazonS3Exception with 5xx are transient.\n            return ex is AmazonS3Exception s3Ex && (int)s3Ex.StatusCode >= It embraces the Observer pattern in order to be\n// embeddable in both streaming (push) and batch (pull) scenarios while\n// still preserving functional purity through a user-supplied\n// aggregation delegate.\n//\n// Key capabilities\n// \u2022 Tumbling & sliding windows                                             \n// \u2022 Thread-safe, lock-free hot path                                        \n// \u2022 Back-pressure aware via System.Threading.Channels                      \n// \u2022 Real-time Observable<KpiMetric> output                                 \n// \u2022 Fault-tolerant (bubble-up strategy / DLQ compatible)                   \n// ---------------------------------------------\n#nullable enable\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Globalization;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Reactive.Linq;\nusing System.Reactive.Subjects;\nusing System.Runtime.CompilerServices;\nusing System.Text.Json;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Channels;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\n\nnamespace PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Single domain event coming from any ingestion source.\n    /// A deliberately flat structure that can be re-shaped downstream.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <param name=\"Timestamp\">UTC timestamp the event occurred.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"EventType\">Human-friendly event discriminator.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"ActorId\">Primary user / system identifier.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"NumericValue\">\n    /// Optional raw measurement (e.g. duration seconds, bytes, \u2026).\n    /// When null the <see cref=\"Attributes\"/> collection must carry meaning.\n    /// </param>\n    /// <param name=\"Attributes\">Catch-all property bag.</param>\n    public sealed record ProductivityEvent(\n        DateTimeOffset Timestamp,\n        string EventType,\n        string ActorId,\n        decimal? NumericValue,\n        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string>? Attributes);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Output of the aggregator \u2013 one atomic KPI.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <param name=\"WindowStart\">Left-inclusive boundary.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"WindowEnd\">Right-exclusive boundary.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"MetricName\">Business-level name (e.g. \"FocusTimeRatio\").</param>\n    /// <param name=\"Value\">Aggregated numeric value.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"DimensionKeys\">Partition keys used for slicing/dicing.</param>\n    public sealed record KpiMetric(\n        DateTimeOffset WindowStart,\n        DateTimeOffset WindowEnd,\n        string MetricName,\n        decimal Value,\n        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string>? window emit points.\n        /// For tumbling windows this acts as window size as well.\n        /// </summary>\n        public required TimeSpan SlideInterval { get; init; }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Whether watermarking (late event allowance) is active.\n        /// </summary>\n        public TimeSpan AllowedLateness { get; init; } = TimeSpan.Zero;\n\n        public TimeWindowType WindowType { get; init; } = TimeWindowType.Tumbling;\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Safety check to avoid mis-configuration at runtime.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentException\"></exception>\n        public void Validate()\n        {\n            if (WindowSize <= TimeSpan.Zero)\n                throw new ArgumentException($\"{nameof(WindowSize)} must be > 0\", nameof(WindowSize));\n\n            if (SlideInterval <= TimeSpan.Zero)\n                throw new ArgumentException($\"{nameof(SlideInterval)} $\"{nameof(SlideInterval)} cannot exceed {nameof(WindowSize)} for sliding windows.\", nameof(SlideInterval));\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Calculates a KPI value from a set of <see metric(s).</returns>\n    public delegate IEnumerable<KpiMetric> KpiAggregationDelegate(\n        IReadOnlyCollection<ProductivityEvent> windowEvents,\n        DateTimeOffset windowStart,\n        DateTimeOffset windowEnd);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Reactive, high-performance aggregation engine.\n    /// Implements IObserver for ingestion and IObservable for metric fan-out.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class TimeSeriesWindowAggregator : IObserver<ProductivityEvent>, IObservable<KpiMetric>, IAsyncDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly KpiAggregationDelegate _aggregationLogic;\n        private readonly TimeWindowOptions _options;\n\n        private readonly Subject<KpiMetric> _metricStream = new();\n        private readonly Channel<ProductivityEvent> _inputChannel;\n\n        // Concurrency primitives\n        private readonly CancellationTokenSource _cts = new();\n        private readonly Task _backgroundTask;\n\n        // Internal buffer storing events inside the current active window(s)\n        // We deliberately use a ConcurrentQueue to keep insertion O(1) and avoid\n        // global locks on the hot path.\n        private readonly ConcurrentQueue<ProductivityEvent> _buffer = new();\n\n        // Latest watermark processed (monotonic)\n        private DateTimeOffset _currentWindowCutoff;\n\n        public TimeSeriesWindowAggregator(\n            KpiAggregationDelegate aggregationLogic,\n            TimeWindowOptions options,\n            int boundedCapacity = 10_000) // backpressure\n        {\n            options.Validate();\n\n            _aggregationLogic = aggregationLogic ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(aggregationLogic));\n            _options = options;\n\n            _inputChannel = Channel.CreateBounded<ProductivityEvent>(new BoundedChannelOptions(boundedCapacity)\n            {\n                SingleReader = true,\n                SingleWriter = false,\n                FullMode = BoundedChannelFullMode.Wait\n            });\n\n            _currentWindowCutoff = AlignToWindowStart(DateTimeOffset.UtcNow);\n\n            _backgroundTask = Task.Factory.StartNew(\n                WorkLoopAsync,\n                _cts.Token,\n                TaskCreationOptions.LongRunning,\n                TaskScheduler.Default).Unwrap();\n        }\n\n        #region IObserver\n\n        public void OnNext(ProductivityEvent value)\n        {\n            if (!_inputChannel.Writer.TryWrite(value))\n            {\n                // backpressure fallback \u2013 should never happen due to boundedChannel Wait\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Input channel rejected write unexpectedly.\");\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void OnError(Exception error)\n        {\n            // Bubble up to downstream subscribers \u2013 they'll decide what to do.\n            _metricStream.OnError(error);\n        }\n\n        public void OnCompleted()\n        {\n            _inputChannel.Writer.Complete();\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        #region IObservable\n\n        public IDisposable Subscribe(IObserver<KpiMetric> observer)\n        {\n            return _metricStream.AsObservable().Subscribe(observer);\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        private async Task WorkLoopAsync()\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                var reader = _inputChannel.Reader;\n\n                while (await reader.WaitToReadAsync(_cts.Token).ConfigureAwait(false))\n                {\n                    while (reader.TryRead(out var evt))\n                    {\n                        _buffer.Enqueue(evt);\n                    }\n\n                    FlushExpiredWindows();\n                }\n            }\n            catch (OperationCanceledException)\n            {\n                // Normal shutdown \u2013 ignore.\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                // Surface unexpected exceptions so ops team is alerted (PagerDuty).\n                _metricStream.OnError(ex);\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                _metricStream.OnCompleted();\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Remove records that no longer belong to any open window and emit\n        /// completed windows downstream.\n        /// </summary>\n        [MethodImpl(MethodImplOptions.AggressiveInlining)]\n        private void FlushExpiredWindows()\n        {\n            var now = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow;\n\n            // Move watermark forward in increments of SlideInterval until the current time is covered.\n            while (_currentWindowCutoff + _options.WindowSize <= now)\n            {\n                var windowStart = _currentWindowCutoff;\n                var windowEnd = windowStart + _options.WindowSize;\n\n                // Gather relevant events.\n                var windowEvents = DrainEvents(windowStart, windowEnd);\n\n                // Apply user-supplied aggregation delegate.\n                try\n                {\n                    foreach (var metric in _aggregationLogic(windowEvents, windowStart, windowEnd))\n                    {\n                        _metricStream.OnNext(metric);\n                    }\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    // Fail-fast on faulty business logic so we don't silently produce wrong numbers.\n                    _metricStream.OnError(new AggregationException(\n                        $\"Aggregation delegate threw for window {windowStart:o}-{windowEnd:o}\", ex));\n                }\n\n                // Advance watermark\n                _currentWindowCutoff = windowStart + _options.SlideInterval;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Retrieve and remove events from the buffer that are part of the\n        /// requested window interval.\n        /// </summary>\n        private IReadOnlyCollection<ProductivityEvent> DrainEvents(DateTimeOffset windowStart, DateTimeOffset windowEnd)\n        {\n            var set = new List<ProductivityEvent>(capacity: 1024);\n\n            while (_buffer.TryPeek(out var candidate))\n            {\n                if (candidate.Timestamp < windowStart)\n                {\n                    // Too old: discard\n                    _buffer.TryDequeue(out _);\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                if (candidate.Timestamp >= windowEnd)\n                {\n                    // Still in future window \u2013 stop draining.\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                // In window range\n                _buffer.TryDequeue(out var inWindow);\n                if (inWindow != null)\n                {\n                    set.Add(inWindow);\n                }\n            }\n\n            return set;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Aligns the given timestamp to the previous aligned window boundary.\n        /// </summary>\n        private DateTimeOffset AlignToWindowStart(DateTimeOffset timestamp)\n        {\n            var ticks = (long)(_options.SlideInterval.Ticks *\n                               Math.Floor(timestamp.UtcTicks / (double)_options.SlideInterval.Ticks));\n            return new DateTimeOffset(ticks, TimeSpan.Zero);\n        }\n\n        public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()\n        {\n            _cts.Cancel();\n\n            // Wait for graceful termination, but don't block forever.\n            var completedTask = await Task.WhenAny(_backgroundTask, Task.Delay(5000)).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            if (completedTask != _backgroundTask)\n            {\n                // Force task to fault for diagnostic purposes\n                _metricStream.OnError(new TimeoutException(\"Aggregator failed to shut down in timely manner.\"));\n            }\n\n            _cts.Dispose();\n            _metricStream.Dispose();\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Aggregation delegate convenience builder that computes a simple\n        /// sum over NumericValue field.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static KpiAggregationDelegate SumNumeric(string metricName, Func<ProductivityEvent, bool>? predicate = null)\n            => (events, start, end) =>\n            {\n                var query = predicate is null ? events : events.Where(predicate);\n                var total = query.Sum(e => e.NumericValue.GetValueOrDefault());\n                return new[]\n                {\n                    new KpiMetric(start, end, metricName, total, DimensionKeys: null)\n                };\n            };\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Bundles aggregation related failures so they can be handled explicitly\n    /// by an upstream error boundary (e.g. Lambda DLQ).\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class AggregationException : Exception\n    {\n        public AggregationException(string message, Exception innerException)\n            : base(message, innerException)\n        {\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Example usage wiring in a Lambda context\n    //\n    // var options = new TimeWindowOptions\n    // {\n    //     WindowSize = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5),\n    //     SlideInterval = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(1)\n    // };\n // aggregator.OnCompleted();\n}\n```",

NullLogger.Instance;\n            using var _ = logger.BeginScope(\"{Kpi}\", Identifier);\n\n            logger.LogDebug(\"Starting KPI computation.\");\n\n            // Filter events that overlap with computation window.\n            var windowEvents = context.CalendarEvents\n                                      .Where(e => e.OverlapsWith(context.WindowStart, context.WindowEnd))\n                                      .ToArray();\n\n            logger.LogDebug(\"Found {Count} overlapping calendar events.\", windowEvents.Length);\n\n            // Compute durations.\n            var focusDuration   = AggregateDuration(windowEvents, CalendarEventType.Focus);\n            var meetingDuration = AggregateDuration(windowEvents, CalendarEventType.Meeting);\n\n            // Defensive checks for cancellation.\n            cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n            double ratio;\n            try\n            {\n                ratio = ComputeRatio(focusDuration, meetingDuration);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex) when (ex is not OperationCanceledException)\n            {\n                logger.LogError(ex, \"Error during ratio computation.\");\n                throw new KpiComputationException(\"Failed to compute Focus-Time Ratio.\", ex);\n            }\n\n            logger.LogInformation(\n                \"Computed Focus-Time Ratio KPI. double.NaN\n                   : focus.TotalSeconds / (focus + meeting).TotalSeconds;\n\n        private static async Task SimulateLatencyAsync(CancellationToken token)\n        {\n            // The real implementation would call feature-flag services or other micro-services.\n            await Task.Delay(5, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Support Types ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>Strongly-typed computation exception for KPI engine.</summary>\n    public sealed class KpiComputationException : Exception\n    {\n        public KpiComputationException(string message, Exception? The engine is used by several\n// Lambda micro-components (stream, batch, CDC) to convert raw telemetry into\n// domain KPIs.  Strategies are resolved through attribute-based discovery and\n// wired via Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection so that teams can\n// hot-swap business logic without re-deploying the outer Lambda shell.\n//\n// AWS SSM is used for real-time feature-flag control, enabling Ops to promote\n// or roll back strategies instantly.  The engine is thread-safe, highly\n// observable, and defensive against poisoned messages.\n//\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Reflection;\nusing System.Text.Json;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Amazon.SimpleSystemsManagement;\nusing Amazon.SimpleSystemsManagement.Model;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations\n{\n    #region Public Contracts\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///   DTO for an incoming pipeline record.  The envelope contains both the\n    ///   raw JSON payload and a set of normalized headers used throughout the\n    ///   warehouse mesh.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record RecordEnvelope(\n        string Stream,               // e.g. \u201cprod/github/push\u201d\n        string SchemaVersion,        // e.g. \u201cv1\u201d\n        DateTimeOffset Timestamp,    // producer timestamp\n        JsonDocument Payload)        // opaque JSON blob\n    {\n        public string TenantId =>\n            Payload.RootElement.TryGetProperty(\"tenantId\", out var t)\n                ? t.GetString() ?? \"unknown\"\n                : \"unknown\";\n\n        /// <summary>Convenience accessor for correlation id.</summary>\n        public string CorrelationId =>\n            Payload.RootElement.TryGetProperty(\"correlationId\", out var c)\n                ? c.GetString() ?? Guid.Empty.ToString()\n                : Guid.Empty.ToString();\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///   Data-transformation strategy abstraction.  Implementations convert a\n    ///   <see cref=\"RecordEnvelope\"/> into the derived KPI representation.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IDataTransformationStrategy\n    {\n        /// <summary>Unique name used during strategy selection (case-insensitive).</summary>\n        string Name { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>Executes the transformation asynchronously.</summary>\n        /// <exception cref=\"TransformationException\">\n        ///   Thrown when a business-rule violation or unrecoverable data\n        ///   inconsistency is detected.\n        /// </exception>\n        Task<JsonElement> TransformAsync(\n            RecordEnvelope envelope,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///   Marker attribute used for automatic strategy discovery through\n    ///   reflection.\n    /// </summary>\n    [AttributeUsage(AttributeTargets.Class)]\n    public sealed class TransformationStrategyAttribute : Attribute\n    {\n        public TransformationStrategyAttribute(string name)\n        {\n            Name = name;\n        }\n\n        public string Name { get; }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>Thrown when transformation processing fails.</summary>\n    public sealed class TransformationException : Exception\n    {\n        public TransformationException(string message, Exception? inner = null)\n            : base(message, inner) { }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Strategy Resolution & Execution Engine\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///   Resolves and executes transformation strategies.        {\n            var strategyTypes =\n                Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly()\n                        .DefinedTypes\n                        .Where(t => !t.IsAbstract\n                                    && typeof(IDataTransformationStrategy).IsAssignableFrom(t)\n                                    && t.GetCustomAttribute<TransformationStrategyAttribute>() is not null)\n                        .ToArray();\n\n            foreach (var type in strategyTypes)\n            {\n                services.AddSingleton(typeof(IDataTransformationStrategy), type);\n                bootstrapLogger?.LogInformation(\n                    \"Registered transformation strategy {StrategyType}\", type.FullName);\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        ///   Entry default)\n        {\n            if (envelope is null)\n                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(envelope));\n\n            var strategy = await ResolveStrategyAsync(envelope.TenantId, cancellationToken);\n            try\n            {\n                return await strategy.TransformAsync(envelope, cancellationToken);\n            }\n            catch (TransformationException tex)\n            {\n                // Business-level exception: send to DLQ with context\n                _logger.LogWarning(tex,\n                    \"Transformation failed (tenant={Tenant}, strategy.Name);\n\n                throw new TransformationException(\n                    $\"Unexpected error executing strategy {strategy.Name}\", ex);\n            }\n        }\n\n        #region Strategy Resolution Internals\n\n        private async Task<IDataTransformationStrategy> ResolveStrategyAsync(\n            string tenant,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n        {\n            var (strategyName, _) =\n                await GetTenantStrategyNameAsync(tenant, cancellationToken);\n\n            if (_strategyCache.TryGetValue(strategyName, out var strategy))\n                return strategy;\n\n            // Strategy not yet cached, resolve through DI\n            strategy = _serviceProvider\n                      .GetServices<IDataTransformationStrategy>()\n                      .FirstOrDefault(s =>\n                          s.Name.Equals(strategyName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));\n\n            if (strategy is null)\n            {\n (_tenantStrategyCache.TryGetValue(tenant, out var entry)\n                && entry.Expires > DateTimeOffset.UtcNow)\n            {\n                return entry;\n            }\n\n            // WithDecryption = false\n                    }, token);\n\n                entry = (response.Parameter.Value, DateTimeOffset.UtcNow + _parameterTtl);\n            }\n            catch occurredAtUtc)\n        {\n            OccurredAtUtc = occurredAtUtc;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>The moment (UTC) when the event occurred in the originating system.</summary>\n        public ------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Defines a pluggable transformation strategy that consumes <see cref=\"DomainEvent\"/>\n    /// instances and IEventSubject<DomainEvent> Subject { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Starts the transformation pipeline.\n        /// Implementations are expected to run until <paramref ValueTask PublishAsync(T domainEvent, CancellationToken ct);\n        void Attach(IEventObserver<T> observer);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Default channel-backed event subject supporting     private readonly IList<IEventObserver<T>> _observers = new List<IEventObserver<T>>();\n        private readonly CancellationTokenSource _internalCts = new();\n        private readonly Task _pumpTask;\n        private readonly ILogger _logger;\n\n        public ChannelEventSubject(int capacity, ILogger logger)\n        {\n            _logger = logger;\n            _channel = Channel.CreateBounded<T>(new BoundedChannelOptions(capacity)\n            {\n                FullMode = BoundedChannelFullMode.Wait,\n                SingleWriter = false,\n                SingleReader = true\n            });\n\n            _pumpTask = Task.Run(() => PumpAsync(_internalCts.Token), _internalCts.Token);\n        }\n\n        public void Attach(IEventObserver<T> observer) => _observers.Add(observer);\n\n        public async ValueTask PublishAsync(T domainEvent, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                await _channel.Writer.WriteAsync(domainEvent, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n            catch (OperationCanceledException) when (ct.IsCancellationRequested)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(\"PublishAsync was cancelled.\");\n                throw;\n            }\n        }\n\n        private async Task PumpAsync(CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            await foreach (var item in _channel.Reader.ReadAllAsync(ct).ConfigureAwait(false))\n            {\n                foreach (var observer in _observers)\n                {\n                    try\n                    {\n                        await observer.OnNextAsync(item, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    }\n                    catch (Exception ex)\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogError(ex, \"Observer {Observer} failed to process event {Event}.\", observer.GetType().Name, item);\n                        // Swallow to ensure other observers still receive the event\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            _internalCts.Cancel();\n            _channel.Writer.Complete();\n            try { _pumpTask.Wait(TimeSpan.FromSeconds(5)); }\n            catch { /* ignored */ }\n            _internalCts.Dispose();\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Concrete Strategy Implementation ---------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Computes Deployment Lead-Time (time between commit push and production deployment).\n    /// Persisted output schema:\n    ///   kpi_name           STRING   (e.g. 'deployment_lead_time')\n    ///   commit_id          STRING\n    ///   repository         STRING\n    ///   environment        STRING\n    /// snapshot_date      DATE     (partition key)\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy : IKpiTransformationStrategy, IEventObserver<DomainEvent>, IDisposable\n    {\n        private const string OutputKpiName = \"deployment_lead_time\";\n        private readonly ILogger _logger;\n        private readonly ChannelEventSubject<DomainEvent> _subject;\n        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, CodeCommitEvent> _commitCache = new(StringComparer.Ordinal);\n        private IAsyncCollector<IDictionary<string, object>>? _sink;\n\n        public DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy(ILogger<DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy> logger, int bufferCapacity = 1_024)\n        {\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n            _subject = new ChannelEventSubject<DomainEvent>(bufferCapacity, logger);\n            _subject.Attach(this);\n        }\n\n        public string Name => OutputKpiName;\n        public IEventSubject<DomainEvent> Subject => _subject;\n\n        public async Task StartAsync(IAsyncCollector<IDictionary<string, object>> sink, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n        {\n            _sink = sink ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(sink));\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy started. Waiting for cancellation\u2026\");\n            try\n            {\n                // Just wait until cancelled. All heavy lifting is event-driven via observers.\n                await Task.Delay(Timeout.Infinite, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n            catch (OperationCanceledException) when (cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)\n            {\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy is shutting down due to cancellation.\");\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                Dispose();\n            }\n        }\n\n        public async ValueTask OnNextAsync(DomainEvent @event, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            switch (@event)\n            {\n                case CodeCommitEvent commit:\n                    HandleCommit(commit);\n                    break;\n\n                case DeploymentEvent deployment:\n                    await HandleDeploymentAsync(deployment, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    break;\n\n                default:\n                    _logger.LogDebug(\"Ignoring unrelated event type {EventType}.\", @event.GetType().Name);\n                    break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        private void HandleCommit(CodeCommitEvent commit)\n        {\n            _commitCache[commit.CommitId] = commit;\n            _logger.LogTrace(\"Cached commit {CommitId} ({Repo}) pushed at {Timestamp}.\",\n                commit.CommitId, commit.Repository, commit.PushedAtUtc);\n        }\n\n        private async Task HandleDeploymentAsync(DeploymentEvent deployment, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            if (!_commitCache.TryRemove(deployment.CommitId, out var commit))\n            {\n                // Commit not seen yet (backfill scenario) \u2014 log and ignore for now.\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Deployment for commit {CommitId} received but commit not found in cache. \" +\n                                        \"Lead-time cannot be computed at this moment.\", deployment.CommitId);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            var leadTime = (deployment.DeployedAtUtc - commit.PushedAtUtc).TotalSeconds;\n            if (leadTime < 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(\"Negative lead-time computed for commit {CommitId}. Pushed at: {Push}, Deployed at: {Deploy}\",\n                    deployment.CommitId, commit.PushedAtUtc, deployment.DeployedAtUtc);\n                // Still record it for further root-cause analysis.\n            }\n\n            var record = new Dictionary<string, object>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)\n            {\n                [\"kpi_name\"]           = OutputKpiName,\n                [\"commit_id\"]          = deployment.CommitId,\n                [\"repository\"]         = commit.Repository,\n                [\"environment\"]        = deployment.Environment,\n                [\"author_email\"]       = commit.AuthorEmail,\n                [\"deployed_by\"]        = deployment.DeployedBy,\n                [\"lead_time_seconds\"]  = leadTime,\n                [\"committed_at_utc\"]   = commit.PushedAtUtc.ToString(\"o\", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),\n                [\"deployed_at_utc\"]    = deployment.DeployedAtUtc.ToString(\"o\", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture),\n                [\"snapshot_date\"]      = deployment.DeployedAtUtc.UtcDateTime.Date.ToString(\"yyyy-MM-dd\", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)\n            };\n\n            if (_sink is null)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(\"Sink has not been initialized. Dropping computed KPI record for commit {CommitId}.\",\n                    deployment.CommitId);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Computed deployment lead-time for commit {CommitId}: {LeadTime}s.\", deployment.CommitId, leadTime);\n\n            try\n            {\n                await _sink.AddAsync(record, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex, \"Failed to persist lead-time KPI for commit {CommitId}.\", deployment.CommitId);\n                // Re-enqueue for retry? For this module, we simply log.\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Disposing DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy and flushing cached commits (count={Count}).\", _commitCache.Count);\n            _subject.Dispose();\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

    "content": "    /// <summary>\n    /// High-level orchestrator that fans-out raw events to the relevant strategy,\n    /// executes them in parallel with retry semantics, and fans-in KPI records.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class TransformationEngine\n    {\n        private static readonly AsyncRetryPolicy RetryPolicy = Policy\n            .Handle<Exception>(ex => ex is not OperationCanceledException)\n            .WaitAndRetryAsync(\n                retryCount: 3,\n                sleepDurationProvider: attempt => TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(100 * Math.Pow(2, attempt)), // 100ms, 200ms, 400ms\n                onRetry: (ex, ts, attempt, ctx) =>\n                {\n                    if (ctx.TryGetValue(\"Logger\", out var obj) && obj is ILogger logger)\n                    {\n                        logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                            \"Transient failure executing strategy (attempt {Attempt}/3). Retrying after {Delay}ms\u2026\",\n                            attempt, ts.TotalMilliseconds);\n                    }\n                });\n\n        private readonly TransformationStrategyRegistry _registry;\n        private readonly ILogger<TransformationEngine> _logger;\n\n        public TransformationEngine(\n            TransformationStrategyRegistry registry,\n            ILogger<TransformationEngine> logger)\n        {\n            _registry = registry ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(registry));\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Orchestrates transformation of a batch of raw events.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task<IReadOnlyCollection<KpiRecord>> ExecuteBatchAsync(\n            IReadOnlyCollection<RawEvent> events,\n            CancellationToken token = default)\n        {\n            if (events is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(events));\n\n            var kpiBag = new ConcurrentBag<KpiRecord>();\n            var stopwatch = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n            // Run transformations concurrently but keep within sane parallelism to protect lambda memory\n            await Parallel.ForEachAsync(events, new ParallelOptions\n            {\n                CancellationToken = token,\n                MaxDegreeOfParallelism = Environment.ProcessorCount // auto-scale based on memory\n            }, async (ev, ct) =>\n            {\n                // Strategy resolution (fast dictionary lookup)\n                ITransformationStrategy strategy;\n                try\n                {\n                    strategy = _registry.GetOrThrow(ev.EventType);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Unable to find strategy for event type '{EventType}'. Dropping event.\", ev.EventType);\n                    return; // swallow \u2013 DLQ routing handled upstream\n                }\n\n                // Execute with retry & jitter\n                var context = new Context().With(\"Logger\", _logger);\n                var results = await RetryPolicy.ExecuteAsync(\n                    (_, _) => strategy.TransformAsync(ev, ct),\n                    context, ct);\n\n                foreach (var kpi in results)\n                {\n                    kpiBag.Add(kpi);\n                }\n            });\n\n            stopwatch.Stop();\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"Processed {EventCount} event(s) into {KpiCount} KPI record(s) in {ElapsedMs} ms.\",\n                events.Count, kpiBag.Count, stopwatch.ElapsedMilliseconds);\n\n            return kpiBag.ToArray();\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Sample Strategies \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Calculates focus-time ratio from calendar events.\n    /// EventType = \"calendar_event\"\n    ///\n    /// Expects payload form:\n    /// {\n    ///     \"start\": \"2024-04-01T09:00:00Z\",\n    ///     \"end\":   \"2024-04-01T10:00:00Z\",\n    ///     \"isRecurring\": false,\n    ///     \"organizer\": \"jane@example.com\",\n    ///     \"attendees\": 9\n    /// }",

Exceptions are surfaced\n        ///     after retries so that upstream Lambda error handling can route\n        ///     to DLQ, yet observers are still notified of failure.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task<KpiResult> ExecuteAsync(\n            TransformationContext context,\n            CancellationToken token = default)\n        {\n            var transformer = _factory.Resolve(context.TargetKpi);\n\n            try\n            {\n                var kpiResult = await RetryPolicy\n                    .WithPolicyKey(\"transformation.retry\")\n                    .ExecuteAsync(\n                        async (ctx, t) =>\n                        {\n                            _logger.LogDebug(\n                                \"Executing transformer {Transformer}\",\n                                transformer.GetType().Name);\n\n                            return await transformer.TransformAsync(context, t)\n                                .ConfigureAwait(false);\n                        },\n                        new Context { [\"logger\"] = _logger },\n                        token);\n\n                await NotifySuccessAsync(kpiResult, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                return kpiResult;\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                await NotifyErrorAsync(ex, context, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                _logger.LogError(ex,\n                    \"Transformation failed for KPI {Kpi}. Context hash: {Hash}\",\n                    context.TargetKpi,\n                    context.GetHashCode());\n\n                // Re-throw so that AWS Lambda or Step Functions\n                // supervisors can route to DLQ automatically.\n                throw;\n            }\n        }\n\n        private Task NotifySuccessAsync(KpiResult result, CancellationToken token)\n        {\n            return Task.WhenAll(_observers.Select(\n                obs => SafeInvokeAsync(() => obs.OnSuccessAsync(result, token))));\n        }\n\n        private Task NotifyErrorAsync(\n            Exception ex, TransformationContext ctx, CancellationToken token)\n        {\n            return Task.WhenAll(_observers.Select(\n                obs => SafeInvokeAsync(() => obs.OnErrorAsync(ex, ctx, token))));\n        }",

cref=\"InvalidOperationException\"/>\n        ///     if the variable is not set or is empty. Intended to centralise defensive checks.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"key\">Name of the environment variable to resolve.</param>\n        /// <returns>Resolved environment variable value.</returns>\n        /// <exception cref=\"InvalidOperationException\">\n        ///     Thrown when the environment variable is missing or empty.\n        /// </exception>\n        public static string RequireEnv(string key)\n        {\n            var value = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(key);\n            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))\n            {\n                throw new InvalidOperationException($\"Required environment variable '{key}' is missing or empty.\");\n            }\n\n            return value;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        ///     Convenience overload that returns <paramref name=\"fallback\"/> when the variable\n        ///     is not set, avoiding an exception for non-critical defaults.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static string GetEnv(string key, string fallback) =>\n            string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(key))\n                ? fallback\n                : Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(key)!;\n\n        /// <summary>\n        ///     Converts the stage (dev|staging|prod) string into a strongly-typed enum.\n        ///     Defensive by design: an unrecognised stage will raise an exception early.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static DeploymentStage GetDeploymentStage()\n        {\n            var stage = RequireEnv(Env.Stage).ToLowerInvariant();\n            return stage switch\n            {\n                \"dev\"     => DeploymentStage.Dev,\n                \"staging\" => DeploymentStage.Staging,\n                \"prod\"    => DeploymentStage.Prod,\n                _ => throw new InvalidOperationException(\n                    $\"Unsupported deployment stage '{stage}'.        Span<byte> buffer    = payload;\n\n            if (!payload.TryCopyTo(hash)) // Rare path \u2014 very large payload, rent array\n            {\n                rented  = true;\n i < chunkSize && enumerator.MoveNext(); i++)\n                    batch.Add(enumerator.Current);\n\n                yield return batch;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Consumes an async sequence (or API that returns Task<IEnumerable{T}>) page-by-page\n        /// and aggregates the items into <paramref name=\"buffer\"/> until the <paramref name=\"predicate\"/> returns <c>false</c>.\n        /// A typical use-case is DynamoDB paginate-until-consumed pattern.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static async Task<List<T>> CollectWhileAsync<T>(\n            Func<string?, Task<(IReadOnlyList<T> Page, string? NextToken)>> pageLoader,\n            Predicate<T> predicate,\n            List<T>? buffer = null,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            buffer ??= new List<T>();\n\n            string? token = null;\n\n            do\n            {\n                ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n                var (page, next) = await pageLoader(token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                foreach (var item in page)\n                {\n                    if (!predicate(item))\n                        return buffer;\n\n                    buffer.Add(item);\n                }\n\n                token = next;\n            }\n            while (token is not null);\n\n            return buffer;\n        }\n        #endregion\n\n        #region ---------- TIME ----------\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Floors the given <see cref=\"DateTime\"/> down to the nearest minute boundary.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static DateTime FloorToMinute(this DateTime dt) =>\n            new(dt.Ticks - (dt.Ticks % TimeSpan.TicksPerMinute), DateTimeKind.Utc);\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Floors the given <see cref=\"DateTime\"/> down by <paramref name=\"quantum\"/> interval.\n        /// Commonly used to bucket temporal metrics (e.g., 5-minute focus windows).\n        /// </summary>\n        public static DateTime Floor(this DateTime dt, TimeSpan quantum)\n        {\n            if (dt.Kind != DateTimeKind.Utc)\n                dt = dt.ToUniversalTime();\n\n            long ticks = dt.Ticks / quantum.Ticks * quantum.Ticks;\n            return new DateTime(ticks, DateTimeKind.Utc);\n        }\n        #endregion\n    }\n}\n```",

public static class ResilienceHelper\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Executes an asynchronous operation with exponential backoff retry strategy.\n        /// The retry policy is configured via <see cref=\"PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_MAX_RETRIES\"/>\n        /// and <see cref=\"PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS\"/>.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <typeparam name=\"T\">The return type of the asynchronous operation.</typeparam>\n        /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>\n        /// <returns>The result of the asynchronous operation.</returns>\n        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentNullException\">Thrown when <paramref name=\"operation\"/> is null.</exception>\n        /// <exception cref=\"Exception\">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>\n        /// <remarks>\n        /// The method implements exponential backoff where the delay between attempts doubles\n        /// with each retry: delay = API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS * 2^attempt (0-indexed).\n        /// Transient exceptions (HttpRequestException, TimeoutException, WebException, and\n        /// AmazonServiceException with 5xx status codes) are retried up to API_MAX_RETRIES times.\n        /// </remarks>\n        public static async Task<T> ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>(\n            Func<Task<T>> operation,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (operation == null)\n                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));\n\n            var maxRetries = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_MAX_RETRIES;\n            var initialBackoffMs = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS;\n\n            Exception? lastException = null;\n\n            for (int attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                    return await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n                catch (OperationCanceledException) when (cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)\n                {\n                    // Cancellation requested \u2014 do not retry, propagate immediately\n                    throw;\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransientException(ex) && attempt < maxRetries)\n                {\n                    lastException = ex;\n\n                    // Calculate exponential backoff delay: initialBackoffMs * 2^attempt\n                    var delayMs = initialBackoffMs * (int)Math.Pow(2, attempt);\n                    await Task.Delay(delayMs, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    // Non-transient exception or final attempt \u2014 propagate\n                    lastException = ex;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n\n            // All retries exhausted \u2014 re-throw the last exception\n            throw lastException!;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Executes an asynchronous operation (no return value) with exponential backoff retry strategy.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>\n        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentNullException\">Thrown when <paramref name=\"operation\"/> is null.</exception>\n        /// <exception cref=\"Exception\">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>\n        public static async Task ExecuteWithRetryAsync(\n            Func<Task> operation,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (operation == null)\n                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));\n\n            // Wrap the void-returning operation in a Task<bool> and         "+",
        "+    /// <summary>",
        "+    /// Centralised resilience helper for executing asynchronous operations with exponential backoff retry.",
        "+    /// Uses configuration constants from <see cref=\"PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants\"/>.",
        "+    /// </summary>",
        "+    public static class ResilienceHelper",
        "+    {",
        "+        /// <summary>",
        "+        /// Executes an asynchronous operation with exponential backoff retry strategy.",
        "+        /// The retry policy is configured via <see cref=\"PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_MAX_RETRIES\"/>",
        "+        /// and <see cref=\"PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS\"/>.",
        "+        /// </summary>",
        "+        /// <typeparam name=\"T\">The return type of the asynchronous operation.</typeparam>",
        "+        /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>",
        "+        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>",
        "+        /// <returns>The result of the asynchronous operation.</returns>",
        "+        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentNullException\">Thrown when <paramref name=\"operation\"/> is null.</exception>",
        "+        /// <exception cref=\"Exception\">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>",
        "+        /// <remarks>",
        "+        /// The method implements exponential backoff where the delay between attempts doubles",
        "+        /// with each retry: delay = API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS * 2^attempt (0-indexed).",
        "+        /// Transient exceptions (HttpRequestException, TimeoutException, WebException, and",
        "+        /// AmazonServiceException with 5xx status codes) are retried up to API_MAX_RETRIES times.",
        "+        /// </remarks>",
        "+        public static async Task<T> ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>(",
        "+            Func<Task<T>> operation,",
        "+            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)",
        "+        {",
        "+            if (operation == null)",
        "+                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));",
        "+",
        "+            var maxRetries = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_MAX_RETRIES;",
        "+            var initialBackoffMs = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS;",
        "+",
        "+            Exception? lastException = null;",
        "+",
        "+            for (int attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++)",
        "+            {",
        "+                try",
        "+                {",
        "+                    cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();",
        "+                    return await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);",
        "+                }",
        "+                catch (OperationCanceledException) when (cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)",
        "+                {",
        "+                    // Cancellation requested \u2014 do not retry, propagate immediately",
        "+                    throw;",
        "+                }",
        "+                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransientException(ex) && attempt < maxRetries)",
        "+                {",
        "+                    lastException = ex;",
        "+",
        "+                    // Calculate exponential backoff delay: initialBackoffMs * 2^attempt",
        "+                    var delayMs = initialBackoffMs * (int)Math.Pow(2, attempt);",
        "+                    await Task.Delay(delayMs, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);",
        "+                }",
        "+                catch (Exception ex)",
        "+                {",
        "+                    // Non-transient exception or final attempt \u2014 propagate",
        "+                    lastException = ex;",
        "+                    break;",
        "+                }",
        "+            }",
        "+",
        "+            // All retries exhausted \u2014 re-throw the last exception",
        "+            throw lastException!;",
        "+        }",
        "+",
        "+        /// <summary>",
        "+        /// Executes an asynchronous operation (no return value) with exponential backoff retry strategy.",
        "+        /// </summary>",
        "+        /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>",
        "+        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>",
        "+        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentNullException\">Thrown when <paramref name=\"operation\"/> is null.</exception>",
        "+        /// <exception cref=\"Exception\">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>",
        "+        public static async Task ExecuteWithRetryAsync(",
        "+            Func<Task> operation,",
        "+            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)",
        "+        {",
        "+            if (operation == null)",
        "+                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));",
        "+",
        "+            // Wrap the void-returning operation in a Task<bool> and delegate to the generic method",
        "+            await ExecuteWithRetryAsync(async () =>",
        "+            {",
        "+                await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);",
        "+                return true;",
        "+            }, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);",
        "+        }",
        "+",
        "+        /// <summary>",
        "+        /// Determines whether an exception is considered transient and should be retried.",
        "+        /// </summary>",
        "+        /// <param name=\"exception\">The exception to evaluate.</param>",
        "+        /// <returns><c>true</c> if the exception is transient; otherwise, <c>false</c>.</returns>",
        "+        private static bool IsTransientException(Exception exception)",
        "+        {",
        "+            return exception switch",
        "+            {",
        "+                System.Net.Http.HttpRequestException => true,",
        "+                TimeoutException => true,",
        "+                WebException => true,",
        "+                AmazonServiceException ase when",
        "+                    ase.StatusCode is HttpStatusCode.InternalServerError",
        "+                                   or HttpStatusCode.BadGateway",
        "+                                   or HttpStatusCode.ServiceUnavailable",
        "+                                   or HttpStatusCode.GatewayTimeout",
        "+                                   or HttpStatusCode.TooManyRequests => true,",
        "+                _ => false",
        "+            };",
        "+        }",
        "+    }",
        " }",

public static class ResilienceHelper\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Executes an asynchronous operation with exponential backoff retry strategy.\n        /// The retry policy is configured
