</summary>\n        /// <typeparam name=\"T\">The return type of the asynchronous operation.</typeparam>\n        /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>\n        /// <returns>The result of the asynchronous operation.</returns>\n        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentNullException\">Thrown when <paramref name=\"operation\"/> is null.</exception>\n        /// <exception cref=\"Exception\">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>\n        /// <remarks>\n        /// The method implements exponential backoff where the delay between attempts doubles\n        /// with each retry: delay = API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS * 2^attempt (0-indexed).\n        /// Transient exceptions (HttpRequestException, TimeoutException, WebException, and\n        /// AmazonServiceException with 5xx status codes) are retried up to API_MAX_RETRIES times.\n        /// </remarks>\n        public static async Task<T> ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>(\n            Func<Task<T>> operation,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (operation == null)\n                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));\n\n            var maxRetries = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_MAX_RETRIES;\n            var initialBackoffMs = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS;\n\n            Exception? lastException = null;\n\n            for (int attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                    return await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n                catch (OperationCanceledException) when (cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)\n                {\n                    // Cancellation requested \u2014 do not retry, propagate immediately\n                    throw;\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransientException(ex) && attempt < maxRetries)\n                {\n                    lastException = ex;\n\n                    // Calculate exponential backoff delay: initialBackoffMs * 2^attempt\n                    var delayMs = initialBackoffMs * (int)Math.Pow(2, attempt);\n                    await Task.Delay(delayMs, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    // Non-transient exception or final attempt \u2014 propagate\n                    lastException = ex;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n\n            // All retries exhausted \u2014 re-throw the last exception\n            throw lastException!;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Executes an asynchronous operation (no return value) with exponential backoff retry strategy.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>\n        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentNullException\">Thrown when <paramref name=\"operation\"/> is null.</exception>\n        /// <exception cref=\"Exception\">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>\n        public static async Task ExecuteWithRetryAsync(\n            Func<Task> operation,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (operation == null)\n                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));\n\n            // Wrap the void-returning operation in a Task<bool> and delegate to the generic method\n            await ExecuteWithRetryAsync(async () =>\n            {\n                await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                return true;\n            }, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Determines whether an exception is considered transient and should be retried.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"exception\">The exception to evaluate.</param>\n        /// <returns><c>true</c> if the exception is transient; otherwise, <c>false</c>.</returns>\n        private static bool IsTransientException(Exception exception)\n        {\n            return exception switch\n            {\n                System.Net.Http.HttpRequestException => true,\n                TimeoutException => true,\n                WebException => true,\n                AmazonServiceException ase when\n                    ase.StatusCode is HttpStatusCode.InternalServerError\n                                   or HttpStatusCode.BadGateway\n                                   or HttpStatusCode.ServiceUnavailable\n                                   or HttpStatusCode.GatewayTimeout\n                                   or HttpStatusCode.TooManyRequests => true,\n                _ => false\n            };\n        }\n    }\n}\n```",

  "originalFile": "```csharp\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//  Project : PulseOps Warehouse \u2014 Serverless Productivity Intelligence Fabric\n//  File    : module_10.txt   (implementation only; filename is controlled by build pipeline)\n//  License : MIT\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//  Description\n//  ------------\n//  Transformation module that materialises productivity-oriented KPIs from a heterogenous event feed.\n//  Implements the Strategy-Pattern so that additional KPIs can be plugged in without redeploying the\n//  compute units.  The module is designed to execute inside an AWS Lambda but is consciously decoupled\n//  from the hosting environment (no direct dependency on Amazon.Lambda.* packages) so it can also be\n//  reused by Glue, Fargate, or on-prem batch jobs.\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\n\nusing Amazon.S3;\nusing Amazon.S3.Model;\n\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations\n{\n    #region Public DTOs / Contracts -----------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Thin wrapper around any raw event that enters the warehouse.\n    /// Envelopes allow us to standardise metadata required for transformation,\n    /// without rewriting every single ingestion lambda when an attribute is added later on.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <remarks>\n    /// The schema mirrors the one emitted by the <c>EventIngressProcessor</c> lambda.\n    /// </remarks>\n    public sealed record EventEnvelope\n    {\n        public required string EventId          { get; init; }\n        public required IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> Dimensions      { get; init; }\n        public          IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string>? AdditionalMeta { get; init; }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Contract for a pluggable KPI strategy.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IKpiCalculationStrategy\n    {\n        /// <summary>Name of the KPI \u2013 MUST be unique.</summary>\n        string KpiName { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>Returns <c>true</c> if the strategy can handle the given event.</summary>\n        bool CanHandle(EventEnvelope envelope);\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Performs calculation and yields one or more KPI rows. -------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Coordinates incoming event stream and dispatches to registered KPI strategies.\n    /// Takes care of parallelism, back-pressure, exception isolation, and durability (S3 write).\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class KpiTransformationEngine : IAsyncDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly IReadOnlyList<IKpiCalculationStrategy> _strategies;\n        private readonly IS3KpiWriter                           _writer;\n        private readonly ILogger<KpiTransformationEngine>       _logger;\n        private readonly SemaphoreSlim                          _parallelism;\n\n        public KpiTransformationEngine(\n            IEnumerable<IKpiCalculationStrategy> strategies,\n            IS3KpiWriter                           writer,\n            ILogger<KpiTransformationEngine>       logger,\n            int                                    maxDegreeOfParallelism = 8)\n        {\n            _strategies   = strategies?.ToList() ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategies));\n            _writer       = writer     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(writer));\n            _logger       = logger     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n            if (!_strategies.Any())\n                throw new ArgumentException(\"At least one KPI strategy must be provided.\", nameof(strategies));\n\n            _parallelism  = new SemaphoreSlim(maxDegreeOfParallelism, maxDegreeOfParallelism);\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Orchestrates transformation for a batch of events.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async ValueTask ExecuteAsync(\n            IEnumerable<EventEnvelope> events,\n            CancellationToken         ct = default)\n        {\n            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(events);\n\n            var tasks = new List<Task>();\n\n            foreach (var envelope in events)\n            {\n                await _parallelism.WaitAsync(ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                // Fire-and-forget \u2013 safe because we await all tasks in the list below\n                tasks.Add(Task.Run(async () =>\n                {\n                    try\n                    {\n                        await DispatchToStrategiesAsync(envelope, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    }\n                    catch (Exception ex)\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogError(ex,\n                            \"Uncaught exception while processing event {EventId}. \" +\n                            \"The event will be re-queued to the DLQ by the Lambda runtime.\",\n                            envelope.EventId);\n                        // Bubble up to trigger Lambda DLQ \u2013 do NOT swallow\n                        throw;\n                    }\n                    finally\n                    {\n                        _parallelism.Release();\n                    }\n                }, ct));\n            }\n\n            await Task.WhenAll(tasks).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n\n        private async Task DispatchToStrategiesAsync(EventEnvelope envelope, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            var sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n            var interestedStrategies = _strategies.Where(s => s.CanHandle(envelope)).ToArray();\n            if (interestedStrategies.Length == 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"No KPI strategy registered for event {EventType}.\", envelope.EventType);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            var kpiRows = new ConcurrentBag<KpiCalculationResult>();\n\n            // Parallel but limited to #strategies so trivial overhead\n            var strategyTasks = interestedStrategies.Select(async strategy =>\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    var rows = await strategy.ProcessAsync(envelope, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    foreach (var row in rows) kpiRows.Add(row);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                        \"Strategy {KpiStrategy} failed while processing EventId={EventId}. Skipping strategy.\",\n                        strategy.KpiName, envelope.EventId);\n                }\n            });\n\n            await Task.WhenAll(strategyTasks).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            // Commit results to the Data Lake (S3, parquet files partitioned by YYYY/MM/DD)\n            if (kpiRows.Count > 0)\n            {\n                await _writer.WriteAsync(kpiRows, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"Processed EventId={EventId} in {ElapsedMs:n0} ms with {RowCount} KPI rows.\",\n                envelope.EventId, sw.ElapsedMilliseconds, kpiRows.Count);\n        }\n\n        public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()\n        {\n            _parallelism?.Dispose();\n            if (_writer is IAsyncDisposable asyncDisposable)\n                await asyncDisposable.DisposeAsync().ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Strategy Implementations ----------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Calculates the ratio between focus time and total working hours on a per-user, per-day basis.\n    /// Source events:\n    ///   - CalendarEventCreated / Updated\n    ///   - WorkSessionStarted / Ended (emitted by IDE plugins, CLI wrappers, browser extensions, \u2026)\n    /// </summary>\n    internal sealed class FocusTimeRatioStrategy : IKpiCalculationStrategy\n    {\n        private const string CalendarEventType = \"CalendarEvent\";\n        private const string WorkSessionType   = \"WorkSession\";\n\n        public string KpiName => \"focus_time_ratio\";\n\n        public bool CanHandle(EventEnvelope envelope)\n            => envelope.EventType is CalendarEventType or WorkSessionType;\n\n        public async ValueTask<IEnumerable<KpiCalculationResult>> ProcessAsync(\n            EventEnvelope   envelope,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            // NOTE: In a real-world scenario, we would use a distributed cache (e.g., DAX or Redis)\n            //       to store partial aggregates.  For brevity, this implementation simply returns\n            //       an immediate KPI row when sufficient information is present on the event itself.\n\n            if (envelope.EventType == WorkSessionType &&\n                envelope.Metadata.TryGetValue(\"DurationMinutes\", out var durationStr) &&\n                int.TryParse(durationStr, out var durationMinutes))\n            {\n                var userId = envelope.Metadata[\"UserId\"]!;\n                var date   = envelope.Created.UtcDateTime.Date;\n\n                var result = new KpiCalculationResult\n                {\n                    KpiName        = KpiName,\n                    WindowStartUtc = date,\n                    WindowEndUtc   = date.AddDays(1),\n                    Value          = durationMinutes, // later aggregated to obtain total focus time\n                    Dimensions = new Dictionary<string, string>\n                    {\n                        [\"user_id\"] = userId,\n                        [\"metric\"]  = \"focus_minutes\"\n                    }\n                };\n\n                return new[] { result };\n            }\n\n            if (envelope.EventType == CalendarEventType &&\n                envelope.Metadata.TryGetValue(\"DurationMinutes\", out var calendarDurationStr) &&\n                int.TryParse(calendarDurationStr, out var meetingMinutes))\n            {\n                var userId = envelope.Metadata[\"OrganizerId\"]!;\n                var date   = envelope.Created.UtcDateTime.Date;\n\n                var result = new KpiCalculationResult\n                {\n                    KpiName        = KpiName,\n                    WindowStartUtc = date,\n                    WindowEndUtc   = date.AddDays(1),\n                    Value          = meetingMinutes,\n                    Dimensions = new Dictionary<string, string>\n                    {\n                        [\"user_id\"] = userId,\n                        [\"metric\"]  = \"meeting_minutes\"\n                    }\n                };\n\n                return new[] { result };\n            }\n\n            return Array.Empty<KpiCalculationResult>();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Computes deployment lead-time (commit \u2192 production) on a per-repo basis.\n    /// Maintains a small in-memory buffer which is flushed every <see cref=\"FlushInterval\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    internal sealed class DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy : IKpiCalculationStrategy, IDisposable\n    {\n        private const string CommitEventType     = \"CodeCommitPushed\";\n        private const string ProdDeployEventType = \"CdPipelineDeployed\";\n\n        private readonly TimeSpan                               FlushInterval     = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);\n        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, DateTime> _commitTimestamps = new(StringComparer.Ordinal);\n        private readonly Timer                                  _flushTimer;\n        private readonly ILogger                                _logger;\n\n        public string KpiName => \"deployment_lead_time\";\n\n        public DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy(ILogger<DeploymentLeadTimeStrategy> logger)\n        {\n            _logger      = logger;\n            _flushTimer  = new Timer(_ => FlushExpired(), null, FlushInterval, FlushInterval);\n        }\n\n        public bool CanHandle(EventEnvelope envelope)\n            => envelope.EventType is CommitEventType or ProdDeployEventType;\n\n        public async ValueTask<IEnumerable<KpiCalculationResult>> ProcessAsync(\n            EventEnvelope envelope,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            switch (envelope.EventType)\n            {\n                case CommitEventType:\n                    {\n                        var commitSha  = envelope.Metadata[\"CommitSha\"]!;\n                        _commitTimestamps[commitSha] = envelope.Created.UtcDateTime;\n                        break;\n                    }\n\n                case ProdDeployEventType:\n                    {\n                        var commitSha = envelope.Metadata[\"CommitSha\"]!;\n                        if (_commitTimestamps.TryRemove(commitSha, out var commitTime))\n                        {\n                            var leadTimeMinutes = (envelope.Created.UtcDateTime - commitTime).TotalMinutes;\n                            var repo            = envelope.Metadata[\"Repository\"]!;\n\n                            var kpiRow = new KpiCalculationResult\n                            {\n                                KpiName        = KpiName,\n                                WindowStartUtc = commitTime,\n                                WindowEndUtc   = envelope.Created.UtcDateTime,\n                                Value          = (decimal)leadTimeMinutes,\n                                Dimensions = new Dictionary<string, string>\n                                {\n                                    [\"repository\"] = repo\n                                }\n                            };\n                            return new[] { kpiRow };\n                        }\n                        break;\n                    }\n            }\n\n            return Array.Empty<KpiCalculationResult>();\n        }\n\n        private void FlushExpired()\n        {\n            var threshold = DateTime.UtcNow.AddHours(-24); // assume deploy happens within 24 h\n            foreach (var kvp in _commitTimestamps)\n            {\n                if (kvp.Value < threshold && _commitTimestamps.TryRemove(kvp.Key, out _))\n                {\n                    _logger.LogDebug(\n                        \"Dropped stale commit {CommitSha} for deployment lead-time KPI (older than 24h).\",\n                        kvp.Key);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            _flushTimer.Dispose();\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Persistence Layer -----------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Simple abstraction that serialises KPI rows as ND-JSON and stores them in S3.\n    /// Real-world implementation could write Apache Parquet or Iceberg; ND-JSON keeps demo lightweight.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IS3KpiWriter : IAsyncDisposable\n    {\n        ValueTask WriteAsync(\n            IEnumerable<KpiCalculationResult> rows,\n            CancellationToken                 ct = IS3KpiWriter\n    {\n        private readonly IAmazonS3                 _s3;\n        private readonly string                    _bucket;\n        private readonly ILogger<S3KpiWriter>      _logger;\n\n        private static readonly AmazonS3RetryPolicy RetryPolicy = new();\n\n        public S3KpiWriter(IAmazonS3 s3, string bucket, ILogger<S3KpiWriter> logger)\n        {\n            _s3     = s3     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(s3));\n            _bucket = bucket ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(bucket));\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        public async ValueTask WriteAsync(\n            IEnumerable<KpiCalculationResult> rows,\n            CancellationToken                 ct = default)\n        {\n            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(rows);\n\n            var nowUtc     = DateTime.UtcNow;\n            var partition  = $\"{nowUtc:yyyy/MM/dd}\";\n            var objectKey  = $\"kpi/partition_date={partition}/{Guid.NewGuid():N}.jsonl\";\n\n            // Serialise as ND-JSON\n            var jsonLines  = string.Join('\\n', rows.Select(row => System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(row)));\n\n            var request = new PutObjectRequest\n            {\n                BucketName  = _bucket,\n                Key         = objectKey,\n                ContentBody = jsonLines,\n                ContentType = \"application/json\"\n            };\n\n            await RetryPolicy.ExecuteAsync(\n                async () => await _s3.PutObjectAsync(request, ct).ConfigureAwait(false),\n                ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Wrote {RowCount} KPI rows to s3://{Bucket}/{Key}.\", rows.Count(), _bucket, objectKey);\n        }\n\n        public ValueTask DisposeAsync() => ValueTask.CompletedTask;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Declarative, exponential back-off retry wrapper for S3 operations.\n    /// </summary>\n    internal sealed class AmazonS3RetryPolicy\n    {\n        private static readonly TimeSpan[] BackOffSchedule =\n        {\n            TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(100),\n            TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(250),\n            TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(500),\n            TimeSpan.FromSeconds(1),\n            TimeSpan.FromSeconds(2)\n        };\n\n        public async Task ExecuteAsync(Func<Task> operation, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            var attempt = 0;\n            Exception? lastError = null;\n\n            foreach (var delay in BackOffSchedule.Append(TimeSpan.Zero))\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                    await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    return; // success\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransient(ex))\n                {\n    }\n\n            throw new InvalidOperationException(\n                $\"S3 operation failed after {attempt} retries.\", lastError);\n        }\n\n        private static bool IsTransient(Exception ex)\n        {\n            // TODO: Add richer fault-analysis; for now assume all AmazonS3Exception with 5xx are transient.\n            return ex is AmazonS3Exception s3Ex && (int)s3Ex.StatusCode >= 500;\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

         if (requests == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(requests));\n\n            var requestList = requests.ToList();\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Processing {Count} KPI requests\", requestList.Count);\n\n            var throttler = new SemaphoreSlim(_options.DegreeOfParallelism);\n            var resultCollector = new ConcurrentBag<KpiComputationResult>();\n            var failures = new ConcurrentBag<KpiComputationFailure>();\n\n            var tasks = requestList.Select(async request =>\n            {\n                await                strategy.GetType().Name, request.KpiName);\n\n                        var result = await strategy.ComputeAsync(request, cancellationToken)\n                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        await PersistToLakeAsync(result, cancellationToken)\n                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully processed KPI {Kpi} for Tenant {TenantId}\",\n                            request.KpiName, request.TenantId);\n\n                        resultCollector.Add(result);\n                    }).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex,        await action().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    return; // success\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransient(ex) && attempt <  }\n        }\n\n        private static bool IsTransient(Exception ex)\n        {\n            return ex switch\n            {\n                AmazonServiceException ase\n                    when ase.StatusCode is HttpStatusCode.InternalServerError or HttpStatusCode.ServiceUnavailable => true,\n                TimeoutException => true,\n                _ => false\n            };\n        }\n\n        private async Task PersistToLakeAsync(\n            KpiComputationResult result,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n        {\n            // Example partition:     InputStream = stream,\n                ContentType = \"application/json\",\n                AutoCloseStream = true\n            };\n\n            await _s3Client.PutObjectAsync(putRequest, private (string Bucket, string Key) GetS3LocationForResult(KpiComputationResult result)\n        {\n            var timestamp = result.GeneratedAtUtc;\n            var key =\n                $\"{result.KpiName}/year={timestamp:yyyy}/month={timestamp:MM}/day={timestamp:dd}/hour={timestamp:HH}/{result.TenantId}.json\";\n\n            return (_options.S3Bucket, key);\n        }\n\n   "originalFile": "```csharp\n// File: src/Module64/KpiComputationOrchestrator.cs\n// Project: PulseOps Warehouse \u2014 Serverless Productivity Intelligence Fabric\n//\n// Description:\n//  Implements the Strategy-Pattern based KPI computation orchestrator that runs\n//  inside a Lambda.  The orchestrator resolves a concrete IKpiComputationStrategy\n//  for the requested KPI, fans the work out across multiple threads (or\n//  reserved-concurrency Lambda instances, depending on runtime settings),\n//  handles transient failures with an exponential back-off policy, and finally\n//  streams the normalized result back to the Data-Lake.\n//\n//  The class is intentionally generic and can be reused from both the\n//  stream-processing (real-time) and batch-processing (historical back-fill)\n//  pipelines.\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Net;\nusing System.Text.Json;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Amazon;\nusing Amazon.Runtime;\nusing Amazon.S3;\nusing Amazon.S3.Model;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\nusing PulseOps.Warehouse.Common;\nusing PulseOps.Warehouse.Contracts;\nusing PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations.Strategies;\n\nnamespace PulseOps.Warehouse.Transformations\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Orchestrates KPI computations by delegating the heavy lifting to a pool of\n    /// <see cref=\"IKpiComputationStrategy\"/> implementations.  Responsibilities:\n    ///\n    /// \u2022 Resolve the correct strategy for a given <see cref=\"KpiRequest\"/>\n    /// \u2022 Run the computation across a configurable degree of parallelism\n    /// \u2022 Persist results to the Lake (S3) using a structured partition scheme\n    /// \u2022 Emit CloudWatch observable metrics & traces\n    /// \u2022 Provide robust error-handling / back-off semantics\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class KpiComputationOrchestrator : IKpiComputationOrchestrator\n    {\n        private const string DefaultRegion = \"us-east-1\";\n        private readonly IKpiComputationStrategyRegistry _strategyRegistry;\n        private readonly IAmazonS3 _s3Client;\n        private readonly ILogger<KpiComputationOrchestrator> _logger;\n        private readonly OrchestratorOptions _options;\n\n        public KpiComputationOrchestrator(\n            IKpiComputationStrategyRegistry strategyRegistry,\n            ILogger<KpiComputationOrchestrator> logger,\n            OrchestratorOptions? options = null,\n            IAmazonS3? s3Client = null)\n        {\n            _strategyRegistry = strategyRegistry ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategyRegistry));\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n            _options = options ?? OrchestratorOptions.FromEnvironment();\n            _s3Client = s3Client ?? new AmazonS3Client(FallbackCredentialsFactory.GetCredentials(), RegionEndpoint.GetBySystemName(DefaultRegion));\n        }\n\n        public async Task<KpiBatchResult> ProcessBatchAsync(\n            IEnumerable<KpiRequest> requests,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (requests == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(requests));\n\n            var requestList = requests.ToList();\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Processing {Count} KPI requests\", requestList.Count);\n\n            var throttler = new SemaphoreSlim(_options.DegreeOfParallelism);\n            var resultCollector = new ConcurrentBag<KpiComputationResult>();\n            var failures = new ConcurrentBag<KpiComputationFailure>();\n\n            var tasks = requestList.Select(async request =>\n            {\n                await throttler.WaitAsync(cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                try\n                {\n                    await ExecuteWithRetryAsync(request, cancellationToken, async () =>\n                    {\n                        var strategy = _strategyRegistry.Resolve(request.KpiName);\n                        _logger.LogDebug(\"Resolved strategy {Strategy} for KPI {Kpi}\",\n                            strategy.GetType().Name, request.KpiName);\n\n                        var result = await strategy.ComputeAsync(request, cancellationToken)\n                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        await PersistToLakeAsync(result, cancellationToken)\n                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully processed KPI {Kpi} for Tenant {TenantId}\",\n                            request.KpiName, request.TenantId);\n\n                        resultCollector.Add(result);\n                    }).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Failed to process KPI {Kpi} for Tenant {TenantId}\",\n                        request.KpiName, request.TenantId);\n\n                    failures.Add(new KpiComputationFailure(request, ex));\n                }\n                finally\n                {\n                    throttler.Release();\n                }\n            }).ToArray();\n\n            await Task.WhenAll(tasks).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            return new KpiBatchResult(resultCollector.ToArray(), failures.ToArray());\n        }\n\n        #region Helpers\n\n        private async Task ExecuteWithRetryAsync(\n            KpiRequest request,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken,\n            Func<Task> action)\n        {\n            var attempt = 0;\n            var delay = _options.InitialBackoff;\n\n            while (true)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                    await action().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    return; // success\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransient(ex) && attempt < while processing {Kpi} (Tenant {TenantId}). Retrying in {DelayMs}ms\u2026\",\n                        attempt, _options.MaxRetryAttempts, request.KpiName, request.TenantId, delay.TotalMilliseconds);\n\n                    await ase.StatusCode is HttpStatusCode.InternalServerError or HttpStatusCode.ServiceUnavailable => true,\n                TimeoutException => true,\n                _ => false\n            };\n        }\n\n        private async Task PersistToLakeAsync(\n            KpiComputationResult result,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n        {\n            // Example partition: kpi_name=FocusTimeRatio/year=2023/month=08/day=14/hour=13/<tenantId>.json\n            var (bucket, key) = GetS3LocationForResult(result);\n\n            using var stream =     InputStream = stream,\n                ContentType = \"application/json\",\n                AutoCloseStream = true\n            };\n\n            await _s3Client.PutObjectAsync(putRequest, cancellationToken)\n                .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Persisted KPI {Kpi} result to s3://{Bucket}/{Key}\", result.KpiName, bucket, key);\n        }\n\n        private (string Bucket, string Key) GetS3LocationForResult(KpiComputationResult result)\n        {\n            var timestamp = result.GeneratedAtUtc;\n            var key =\n                $\"{result.KpiName}/year={timestamp:yyyy}/month={timestamp:MM}/day={timestamp:dd}/hour={timestamp:HH}/{result.TenantId}.json\";\n\n            return (_options.S3Bucket, key);\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n\n    #region Options & Contracts\n\n    public sealed record OrchestratorOptions(\n        int DegreeOfParallelism,\n        int MaxRetryAttempts,\n        TimeSpan              double.TryParse(Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(name), out var value) ? value : defaultValue;\n\n            string GetString(string name, string defaultValue) =>\n                Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable(name) ?? defaultValue;\n\n            return new OrchestratorOptions(\n                DegreeOfParallelism: GetInt(\"KPI_DOP\", Environment.ProcessorCount),\n Random.Shared.NextDouble() * 180;\n\n            var ratio = focusMinutes / Math.Max(1, meetingMinutes + focusMinutes);\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Computed Focus-Time Ratio {Ratio:F2} for Tenant {Tenant}\", ratio, request.TenantId);\n\n            return new KpiComputationResult(\n                TenantId: request.TenantId,\n                KpiName: KpiName,\n                WindowStartUtc: request.WindowStartUtc,\n                WindowEndUtc: request.WindowEndUtc,\n                GeneratedAtUtc: DateTimeOffset.UtcNow,\n                Metrics: new Dictionary<string,          });\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Example strategy that calculates Meeting-Cost Index KPI.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class MeetingCostIndexStrategy :         _logger = logger;\n        }\n\n        public string KpiName => \"MeetingCostIndex\";\n\n        public async Task<KpiComputationResult> ComputeAsync(\n            KpiRequest request,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n        {\n            await Task.Delay(TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(100), cancellationToken);\n\n            var averageHourlyRate = 75.0; // USD \u2013 would be looked up from HR data\n            var totalMeetingHours = Random.Shared.NextDouble() * 50;\n            var costIndex = averageHourlyRate * totalMeetingHours;\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Computed Meeting-Cost Index {Cost} for Tenant {Tenant}\", costIndex, request.TenantId);\n\n            return new KpiComputationResult(\n                TenantId:      /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>\n        /// <returns>The result of the asynchronous operation.</returns>\n        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentNullException\">Thrown when <paramref name=\"operation\"/> is null.</exception>\n        /// <exception cref=\"Exception\">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>\n        /// <remarks>\n        /// The method implements exponential backoff where the delay between attempts doubles\n        /// with each retry: delay = API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS * 2^attempt (0-indexed).\n        /// Transient exceptions (HttpRequestException, TimeoutException, WebException, and\n        /// AmazonServiceException with 5xx status codes) are retried up to API_MAX_RETRIES times.\n        /// </remarks>\n        public static async Task<T> ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>(\n            Func<Task<T>> operation,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (operation == null)\n                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));\n\n            var maxRetries = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_MAX_RETRIES;\n            var initialBackoffMs = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS;\n\n            Exception? lastException = null;\n\n            for (int attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                    return await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);\n exception or final attempt \u2014 propagate\n                    lastException = ex;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n\n            // All retries exhausted \u2014 re-throw the last exception\n            throw lastException!;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Executes an asynchronous operation (no return value) with exponential backoff retry strategy.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>\n        /// <exception cref=\"ArgumentNullException\">Thrown when <paramref name=\"operation\"/> is null.</exception>\n        /// <exception cref=\"Exception\">Re-throws the last exception if all retry attempts fail.</exception>\n        public static async Task ExecuteWithRetryAsync(\n            Func<Task> operation,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (operation == null)\n                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));\n\n            // Wrap the operation().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                return true;\n            }, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Determines whether an Refactored module_10.txt - Before (AmazonS3RetryPolicy removed)\n\n```csharp\n// File: /workspace/project_writable/src/module_10.txt (BEFORE)\n// Lines: 435-476 - The entire AmazonS3RetryPolicy class was removed:\n    internal sealed class AmazonS3RetryPolicy\n    {\n        private static readonly TimeSpan[] BackOffSchedule =\n        {\n            TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(100),\n            TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(250),\n            TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(500),\n            TimeSpan.FromSeconds(1),\n            TimeSpan.FromSeconds(2)\n        };\n\n        public async Task ExecuteAsync(Func<Task> operation, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            var attempt = 0;\n            Exception? lastError = null;\n\n            foreach (var delay in BackOffSchedule.Append(TimeSpan.Zero))\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                    await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    return;\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransient(ex))\n                {\n                    lastError = ex;\n                    attempt++;\n                    if (delay > TimeSpan.Zero)\n                        await Task.Delay(delay, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n            }\n\n            throw new InvalidOperationException(\n                $\"S3 operation failed after {attempt} retries.\", lastError);\n        }\n        // ... IsTransient method\n    }\n```\n\n### 4. Refactored module_10.txt - After (Using ResilienceHelper)\n\n```csharp\n// File: /workspace/project_writable/src/module_10.txt (AFTER)\n// Lines: 420-423\n            await PulseOps.Warehouse.Common.ResilienceHelper.ExecuteWithRetryAsync(\n                async () => await _s3.PutObjectAsync(request, ct).ConfigureAwait(false),\n                ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n```\n\n### 5. Refactored module_64.txt - Before (Ad-hoc ExecuteWithRetryAsync removed)\n\n```csharp\n// File: /workspace/project_writable/src/module_64.txt (BEFORE)\n// Lines: 122-160 - The entire ad-hoc retry method was removed:\n        private async Task ExecuteWithRetryAsync(\n            KpiRequest request,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken,\n            Func<Task> action)\n        {\n            var attempt = 0;\n            var delay = _options.InitialBackoff;\n\n            while (true)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                    await action().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    return;\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransient(ex) && attempt < _options.MaxRetryAttempts)\n                {\n                    attempt++;\n                    _logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                        \"[Attempt {Attempt}/{MaxAttempts}] Transient failure...\",\n                        attempt, _options.MaxRetryAttempts, ...);\n\n                    await Task.Delay(delay, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    delay = TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(delay.TotalMilliseconds * _options.BackoffMultiplier);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        private static bool IsTransient(Exception ex)\n        {\n            return ex switch\n            {\n                AmazonServiceException ase\n                    when ase.StatusCode is HttpStatusCode.InternalServerError or HttpStatusCode.ServiceUnavailable => true,\n                TimeoutException => true,\n                _ => false\n            };\n        }\n```\n\n### 6. Refactored module_64.txt - After (Using ResilienceHelper)\n\n```csharp\n// File: /workspace/project_writable/src/module_64.txt (AFTER)\n// Lines: 84-100\n                    await PulseOps.Warehouse.Common.ResilienceHelper.ExecuteWithRetryAsync(async () =>\n                    {\n                        var strategy = _strategyRegistry.Resolve(request.KpiName);\n                        _logger.LogDebug(\"Resolved strategy {Strategy} for KPI {Kpi}\",\n                            strategy.GetType().Name, request.KpiName);\n\n                        var result = await strategy.ComputeAsync(request, cancellationToken)\n                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        await PersistToLakeAsync(result, cancellationToken)\n                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                        _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully processed KPI {Kpi} for Tenant {TenantId}\",\n                            request.KpiName, request.TenantId);\n\n                        resultCollector.Add(result);\n                    }, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Discovery Phase\nI identified ad-hoc retry implementations by searching for common patterns:\n- `HttpRequestException`, `TimeoutException`, `WebException` exception types\n- `Task.Delay` usage patterns\n- `while(true)`, `for` loop retry patterns\n- Variables named `retry`, `attempt`, `maxRetry`\n\n### Key Findings\n\n1. **module_10.txt** - `AmazonS3RetryPolicy` class (lines 435-476)\n   - Implemented a custom retry policy with hardcoded `BackOffSchedule` array\n   - Used a `foreach` loop with `Task.Delay` for exponential backoff\n   - Had its own `IsTransient()` method checking for S3 5xx errors\n\n2. **module_64.txt** - `ExecuteWithRetryAsync` method (lines 122-160)\n   - Implemented a `while(true)` loop with manual retry counting\n   - Used `_options.MaxRetryAttempts` and `_options.InitialBackoff` for configuration\n   - Had its own `IsTransient()` method checking for `AmazonServiceException` and `TimeoutException`\n\n3. **Polly-based implementations** (module_39.txt, module_45.txt, module_68.txt)\n   - These modules already use the Polly library for retry policies\n   - While they have different configurations, they follow a consistent pattern\n   - These were not refactored as they already use a proper resilience library\n\n### Architectural Pattern\nThe refactoring follows the **Strategy Pattern** for error handling:\n- Centralised `ResilienceHelper` class acts as a facade for retry logic\n- Generic `ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>` method accepts any async operation via `Func<Task<T>>`\n- Configuration is pulled from `PulseOpsConstants.API_MAX_RETRIES` and `PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS`\n- Exponential backoff calculation: `delay = API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS * 2^attempt`\n\n## Implementation (Code Modification Task)\n\n### Files Modified\n\n1. **`/workspace/project_writable/src/constants.txt`**\n   - void version\n     - `IsTransientException(Exception)` - transient error detection\n\n3. **`/workspace/project_writable/src/module_10.txt`**\n   - Removed the `AmazonS3RetryPolicy` class (~45 lines)\n   - Removed the private `ExecuteWithRetryAsync()` method (~28 lines)\n   - Removed the private `IsTransient()` method (~10 lines)\n   - Replaced direct method call with `ResilienceHelper.ExecuteWithRetryAsync()`\n\n### Testing / Verification\n- Verified that the constants are correctly defined in constants.txt\n- Confirmed ResilienceHelper is properly implemented with exponential backoff\n- Checked that module_10.txt now uses ResilienceHelper instead of AmazonS3RetryPolicy\n- Checked that module_64.txt now uses ResilienceHelper instead of the local retry method\n- All old retry code artifacts (classes, methods, variables) have been removed\n\n## Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: Successfully centralized and standardized asynchronous operation retry logic across the PulseOps Warehouse codebase by creating a `ResilienceHelper` class with exponential backoff retry semantics.\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - `PulseOpsConstants.API_MAX_RETRIES` (5) - centralized retry count\n  - `PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS` (200ms) - centralized initial backoff\n  - `ResilienceHelper.ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T>()` - generic async retry method\n  - `ResilienceHelper.IsTransientException()` - transient error detection\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: Strategy Pattern with centralized resilience facade. The `ResilienceHelper` class encapsulates the retry policy and can be reused across all modules that need resilient API calls.\n\n- **Files refactored**:\n  - `module_10.txt`: Removed ~45 lines of `AmazonS3RetryPolicy` class\n  - `module_64.txt`: Removed ~38 lines of ad-hoc retry logic\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  - Consider adding logging to `ResilienceHelper` for observability\n  - The existing Polly-based implementations in other modules (module_39, module_45, module_68) could also be migrated to use `ResilienceHelper` for consistency\n  - Consider adding jitter to the exponential backoff to prevent thundering herd issues\n",

</summary>\n        /// <typeparam name=\"T\">The return type of the asynchronous operation.</typeparam>\n        /// <param name=\"operation\">The asynchronous operation to execute with retry semantics.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token for cooperative cancellation.</param>\n        /// <returns>The result of the asynchronous   var initialBackoffMs = PulseOps.Warehouse.Shared.PulseOpsConstants.API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS;\n\n            Exception? lastException = null;\n\n            for (int attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; throw;\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransientException(ex) && attempt < maxRetries)\n                {\n                    lastException = ex;\n                    var delayMs = initialBackoffMs * (int)Math.Pow(2, attempt);\n                    await Task.Delay(delayMs, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    lastException = ex;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n\n            throw lastException!;\n        }\n\n        ///           Func<Task> operation,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (operation == null)\n                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(operation));\n\n            await ExecuteWithRetryAsync(async () =>\n            {\n                await operation().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                return true;\n            }, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n\n        private static bool IsTransientException(Exception exception)\n        {\n            return exception switch\n         // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        // ► Miscellaneous Constants
        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        public static class Misc
        {
            public const int    DefaultTimeoutSeconds     = 30;
            public const string DateTimeFormatIso8601     = "yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.fff'Z'";
            public const string SystemUser                = "pulseops-system@pulseops.io";

        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        // ► API Resilience Configuration
        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        /// <summary>
        ///     Maximum number of retry attempts for transient API failures.
        /// </summary>

4. EDIT /workspace/project_writable/src/utils.txt
Before
        #region ---------- TIME ----------
        /// <summary>
        /// Floors the given <see cref="DateTime"/> down to the nearest minute boundary.
        /// </summary>
        public static DateTime FloorToMinute(this DateTime dt) =>
            new(dt.Ticks - (dt.Ticks % TimeSpan.TicksPerMinute), DateTimeKind.Utc);

        /// <summary>
        /// Floors the given <see cref="DateTime"/> down by <paramref name="quantum"/> interval.
        /// Commonly used to bucket temporal metrics (e.g., 5-minute focus windows).
        /// </summary>
        public static DateTime Floor(this DateTime dt, TimeSpan quantum)
        {
            if (dt.Kind != DateTimeKind.Utc)
                dt = dt.ToUniversalTime();

            long ticks = dt.Ticks / quantum.Ticks * quantum.Ticks;
            return new DateTime(ticks, DateTimeKind.Utc);
        }
        #endregion
    }
}
After
        #region ---------- TIME ----------
        /// <summary>
        /// Floors the given <see cref="DateTime"/> down to the nearest minute boundary.
        /// </summary>
        public static DateTime FloorToMinute(this DateTime dt) =>
            new(dt.Ticks - (dt.Ticks % TimeSpan.TicksPerMinute), DateTimeKind.Utc);

        /// <summary>
        /// Floors the given <see cref="DateTime"/> down by <paramref name="quantum"/> interval.
        /// Commonly used to bucket temporal metrics (e.g., 5-minute focus windows).
        /// </summary>
        public static DateTime Floor(this DateTime dt, TimeSpan quantum)
        {
            if (dt.Kind != DateTimeKind.Utc)
                dt = dt.ToUniversalTime();

            long ticks = dt.Ticks / quantum.Ticks * quantum.Ticks;
            return new DateTime(ticks, DateTimeKind.Utc);
        }
        #endregion
    }

Before
        public async Task<KpiBatchResult> ProcessBatchAsync(
            IEnumerable<KpiRequest> requests,
            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
        {
            if (requests == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(requests));

            var requestList = requests.ToList();
            _logger.LogInformation("Processing {Count} KPI requests", requestList.Count);

            var throttler = new SemaphoreSlim(_options.DegreeOfParallelism);
            var resultCollector = new ConcurrentBag<KpiComputationResult>();
            var failures = new ConcurrentBag<KpiComputationFailure>();

            var tasks = requestList.Select(async request =>
            {
                await throttler.WaitAsync(cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);
                try
                {
                    await ExecuteWithRetryAsync(request, cancellationToken, async () =>
                    {
                        var strategy = _strategyRegistry.Resolve(request.KpiName);
                        _logger.LogDebug("Resolved strategy {Strategy} for KPI {Kpi}",
                            strategy.GetType().Name, request.KpiName);

                        var result = await strategy.ComputeAsync(request, cancellationToken)
                            .ConfigureAwait(false);

                        await PersistToLakeAsync(result, cancellationToken)
                            .ConfigureAwait(false);

                        _logger.LogInformation("Successfully processed KPI {Kpi} for Tenant {TenantId}",
                            request.KpiName, request.TenantId);

                        resultCollector.Add(result);
                    }).ConfigureAwait(false);

# Solution: csharp_data_warehouse_expert_012_cross_file_refactoring_expert_01

## Key Files Identified

- `/workspace/project_writable/src/constants.txt` - Centralized constants file where API_MAX_RETRIES and API_INITIAL_BACKOFF_MS are added
- `/workspace/project_writable/src/utils.txt` - Utilities file where the new ResilienceHelper class with ExecuteWithRetryAsync<T> is implemented
- `/workspace/project_writable/src/module_10.txt` - Contains ad-hoc AmazonS3RetryPolicy class that was refactored
- `/workspace/project_writable/src/module_64.txt` - Contains ad-hoc ExecuteWithRetryAsync method that was refactored
